  (* Definition limArrowOfInverses
             {C : category} {g : graph} {d : diagram g C}
             (CC : LimCone d)
             (c : C) (cc : cone d c)
    : (∏  v : vertex g, is_z_isomorphism (pr1 cc v)) -> is_z_isomorphism (limArrow CC c cc).
  Proof.
    intro iv.
    apply isLim_is_z_iso.
    intros x x_con.
    use tpair.
    - unfold LimCone in CC.
      use tpair.
      + refine (pr11 (pr2 CC x x_con) · _).
        Search lim.
        Search lim.


    use make_is_z_isomorphism.
    - unfold cone in cc.

      Check pr1 cc.
      Search lim. *)

  (∃! g : C ⟦ x, t ⟧, ∏ i0 : I, j i0 · g = t0 i0)

    apply isapropiscontr.
  Qed.

C, D: category
BC: Colims_of_shape two_graph D
F, G: C ⟶ D
nat_z_iso
  (BinCoproduct_of_functors C D
     (BinCoproducts_from_Colims D BC) F G)
  (coproduct_of_functors bool C D
     (Coproducts_from_Colims bool D BC)
     (λ x : bool, if x then F else G))

is_nat_trans
  (BinCoproduct_of_functors C D
     (BinCoproducts_from_Colims D BC) F G)

     (Coproducts_from_Colims bool D BC)
     (λ x : bool, if x then F else G))
  ((λ c : C,
    colimOfArrows
      (BC (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c) (G c)))
      (BC
         (coproducts_diagram bool D
            (λ i : bool,
             (λ x : bool, if x then F else G) i c)))
      (λ b : vertex two_graph,
       bool_rect
         (λ b0 : bool,
          D
          ⟦ dob (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c) (G c))
              b0,
          dob
            (coproducts_diagram bool D
               (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))
            b0 ⟧)
         (identity
            (dob
               (coproducts_diagram bool D
                  (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))
               true))
         (identity
            (dob
               (coproducts_diagram bool D
                  (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))
               false)) b)
      (λ (b1 b2 : vertex two_graph) (e : edge b1 b2),
       fromempty e))
   :
   nat_trans_data

C, D: category
BC: Colims_of_shape two_graph D
F, G: C ⟶ D
is_nat_z_iso
  (make_nat_trans
     (BinCoproduct_of_functors C D
        (BinCoproducts_from_Colims D BC) F G)
     (coproduct_of_functors bool C D
        (Coproducts_from_Colims bool D BC)
        (λ x : bool, if x then F else G))
     ((λ c : C,
       colimOfArrows
         (BC (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c) (G c)))
         (BC
            (coproducts_diagram bool D
               (λ i : bool,
                (λ x : bool, if x then F else G) i c)))
         (λ b : vertex two_graph,
          bool_rect
            (λ b0 : bool,
             D
             ⟦ dob
                 (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c) (G c))
                 b0,
             dob
               (coproducts_diagram bool D
                  (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))
               b0 ⟧)
            (identity
               (dob
                  (coproducts_diagram bool D
                     (λ i : bool,
                      (if i then F else G) c)) true))
            (identity
               (dob
                  (coproducts_diagram bool D
                     (λ i : bool,
                      (if i then F else G) c)) false))
            b)
         (λ (b1 b2 : vertex two_graph)
          (e : edge b1 b2), fromempty e))
      :
      nat_trans_data
        (BinCoproduct_of_functors C D
           (BinCoproducts_from_Colims D BC) F G)
        (coproduct_of_functors bool C D
           (Coproducts_from_Colims bool D BC)
           (λ x : bool, if x then F else G)))
     ((λ (c1 c2 : C) (f : C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧),
       (postcompWithColimArrow
          (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c1) (G c1))
          (BC (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c1) (G c1)))
          (colim
             (BC
                (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c2) (G c2))))
          (BinCoprod D
             (# F f
              · colimIn
                  (BC
                     (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c2)
                        (G c2))) true)
             (# G f
              · colimIn
                  (BC
                     (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c2)
                        (G c2))) false))
          (colim
             (BC
                (coproducts_diagram bool D
                   (λ i : bool,
                    (if i then F else G) c2))))
          (colimOfArrows
             (BC
                (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c2) (G c2)))
             (BC
                (coproducts_diagram bool D
                   (λ i : bool,
                    (if i then F else G) c2)))
             (λ b : bool,
              bool_rect
                (λ b0 : bool,
                 D ⟦ if b0 then F c2 else G c2,
                 (if b0 then F else G) c2 ⟧)
                (identity (F c2)) (identity (G c2)) b)
             (λ (b1 b2 : bool) (e : ∅), fromempty e)) @
        colimArrowUnique
          (BC (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c1) (G c1)))
          (colim
             (BC
                (coproducts_diagram bool D
                   (λ i : bool,
                    (if i then F else G) c2))))
          (make_cocone
             (λ u : vertex two_graph,
              bool_rect
                (λ b : bool,
                 D ⟦ if b then F c1 else G c1,
                 (if b then F else G) c1 ⟧)
                (identity (F c1)) (identity (G c1)) u
              · coconeIn
                  (Coproducts_cocone bool D
                     (colim
                        (BC
                           (coproducts_diagram bool D
                              (...))))
                     (λ i : bool,
                      (if i then F else G) c1)

        (if b0 then F else G) c ⟧) (identity (F c))
       (identity (G c)) b)
    (λ (b1 b2 : bool) (e : ∅), fromempty e)

C, D: category
BC: Colims_of_shape two_graph D
F, G: C ⟶ D
c: C
b: vertex (I_graph bool)
colimIn
  (BC
     (coproducts_diagram bool D
        (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))) b =
bool_rect
  (λ b : bool,
   D ⟦ (if b then F else G) c, if b then F c else G c
   ⟧) (identity (F c)) (identity (G c)) b
· coconeIn
    (make_cocone
       (λ u : vertex two_graph,
        (λ b : bool,
         bool_rect
           (λ b0 : bool,
            D ⟦ if b0 then F c else G c,
            (if b0 then F else G) c ⟧)
           (identity (F c)) (identity (G c)) b) u
        · colimIn
            (BC
               (coproducts_diagram bool D
                  (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c)))
            u)
       (colimOfArrows_subproof D two_graph
          (bincoproduct_diagram D (F c) (G c))
          (coproducts_diagram bool D
             (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c))
          (BC
             (coproducts_diagram bool D
                (λ i : bool, (if i then F else G) c)))
          (λ b : bool,
           bool_rect
             (λ b0 : bool,
              D ⟦ if b0 then F c else G c,
              (if b0 then F else G) c ⟧)
             (identity (F c)) (identity (G c)) b)
          (λ (b1 b2 : bool) (e : ∅), fromempty e))) b

          induction b ; refine (_ @ ! id_left _) ; apply pathsinv0, id_left.
  Defined.

  ((λ b : vertex two_graph,

         × C ⟦ pr1 d false, co ⟧,
isBinCoproduct C (pr1 d true) (pr1 d false)
  (pr1 coiaib) (pr12 coiaib) (pr22 coiaib)
co: C
cc: ∑ f : ∏ v : vertex two_graph, C ⟦ dob d v, co ⟧,
forms_cocone d f
t: ∑ x : C ⟦ pr11 c, co ⟧,
is_cocone_mor
  ((λ b : vertex two_graph,
    bool_rect
      (λ b0 : bool, C ⟦ dob d b0, pr11 c ⟧)
      (pr121 c) (pr221 c) b),,
   (λ (b1 b2 : vertex two_graph) (e : edge b1 b2),
    fromempty e)) cc x
ϕ:= pr1 t,, pr2 t true,, pr2 t false: ∑ fg : C ⟦ pr11 c, co ⟧,
pr121 c · fg = pr1 cc true
× pr221 c · fg = pr1 cc false
p:= pr2 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false)) ϕ: ϕ = pr1 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false))
transportf
  (is_cocone_mor
     ((λ b : vertex two_graph,
       bool_rect (λ b0 : bool, C ⟦ dob d b0, pr11 c ⟧)
         (pr121 c) (pr221 c) b),,
      (λ (b1 b2 : vertex two_graph) (e : edge b1 b2),
       fromempty e)) cc) ?p (pr2 t) =
pr2
  (pr11 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false)),,
   (λ b : vertex two_graph,
    bool_rect
      (λ b0 : bool,
       coconeIn
         ((λ b1 : vertex two_graph,
           bool_rect
             (λ b2 : bool, C ⟦ dob d b2, pr11 c ⟧)
             (pr121 c) (pr221 c) b1),,
          (λ (b1 b2 : vertex two_graph)
           (e : edge b1 b2), fromempty e)) b0
       · pr11 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false)) =
       coconeIn cc b0)
      (pr121 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false)))
      (pr221 (pr2 c co (pr1 cc true) (pr1 cc false)))
      b))

  Definition is_omega_cont_Id_H (H: [C, C] ⟶ [C, C]) :
    is_omega_cont H -> is_omega_cont (Id_H H)
    := is_omega_cont_Const_plus_H (functor_identity C) H.

Section MBindingSig.

Context (sort : UU) (* (Hsort_set : isaset sort) *) (Hsort : isofhlevel 3 sort) (C : category).

(* Assumptions on [C] used to construct the functor *)
(* Note that there is some redundancy in the assumptions *)
Context (TC : Terminal C) (IC : Initial C)
          (BP : BinProducts C) (BC : BinCoproducts C)
          (PC : forall (I : UU), Products I C) (CC : forall (I : UU), isaset I → Coproducts I C).

Local Notation "'1'" := (TerminalObject TC).
Local Notation "a ⊕ b" := (BinCoproductObject (BC a b)).

(* Let Hsort := hlevelntosn 2 _ Hsort_set. *)

(** Define the category of sorts *)
Let sort_cat : category := path_pregroupoid sort Hsort.

(** This represents "sort → C" *)
Let sortToC : category := SortIndexing.sortToC sort Hsort C.

Let BCsortToC : BinCoproducts sortToC := SortIndexing.BCsortToC sort Hsort _ BC.

(* Assumptions needed to prove ω-continuity of the functor *)
Context (HcoC : Lims_of_shape conat_graph C)
 (* (HCcommuteBP : propcoproducts_commute_binproducts C BP (λ p : hProp, CC p (isasetaprop (pr2 p)))) *)
 (HCcommuteCC : ∏ I : SET, ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts C I HcoC (CC (pr1 I) (pr2 I))).



(** * Construction of a monad from a multisorted signature *)
Section monad.

  Local Definition sortToC2 := SortIndexing.sortToC2 sort Hsort C.

  Local Definition sortToC3 := SortIndexing.sortToC3 sort Hsort C.

  Let BCsortToC2 : BinCoproducts sortToC2 := SortIndexing.BCsortToC2 sort Hsort _ BC.

  Let TsortToC2 : Terminal sortToC2 := SortIndexing.TsortToC2 sort Hsort _ TC.

  Local Definition HcoCsortToC : Lims_of_shape conat_graph sortToC := SortIndexing.LLsortToC sort Hsort C conat_graph HcoC.

  Local Definition HcoCsortToC2 : Lims_of_shape conat_graph sortToC2 := SortIndexing.LLsortToC2 sort Hsort C conat_graph HcoC.

  Local Definition MultiSortedSigToFunctor' : MultiSortedSig sort -> sortToC3 := MultiSortedSigToFunctor' sort Hsort C TC BP BC CC.

  Local Definition is_omega_cont_MultiSortedSigToFunctor' (M : MultiSortedSig sort) :
    is_omega_cont (MultiSortedSigToFunctor' M) :=
    is_omega_cont_MultiSortedSigToFunctor' sort Hsort C TC
                                          BP BC CC HcoC HCcommuteCC M.

  Local Definition MultiSortedSigToStrength' : ∏ M : MultiSortedSig sort,
        MultiSorted_actegorical.pointedstrengthfromselfaction_CAT sort Hsort C (MultiSortedSigToFunctor' M)
    := MultiSortedSigToStrength' sort Hsort C TC BP BC CC.

  Let Id_H : sortToC3 → sortToC3 := Id_H sortToC BCsortToC.

  (** Construction of terminal coalgebra for the omega-continuous signature functor with lax lineator *)
